function sr_menus_setupMainNav_button_inline () {
    if (sr_detect_operaMini || !("classList" in document.createElement("_"))) {
	return false;
    }
    var nav_trigger = document.getElementById('nav_trigger');
    if(!nav_trigger || !Modernizr.is_modern || nav_trigger.triggered) {
	return false;
    }
    nav_trigger.triggered = true;
    var nav = document.getElementById('nav');
    var nav_trigger_a = nav_trigger.querySelector('a');
    if (nav_trigger_a) {
	nav_trigger_a.setAttribute('href','javascript:void(0)');
	nav_trigger.onclick = function (event) {
	    nav.classList.toggle('open');
	    var is_open = nav.classList.contains('open');
	    if (is_open) {
		nav_trigger.classList.add('open');
	    }
	    else {
		nav_trigger.classList.remove('open');
	    }
	    event.preventDefault();
	    try { sr_record_analytics_event('MainNavButtonClick_inline',sr_record_directory(),sr_record_page());}
	    catch(err) {}
	};
    }
    return true;
}
sr_menus_setupMainNav_button_inline();

<div class="section_heading">
  <span class="section_anchor" id="pitching_value_link" data-label="Player Value--Pitching"></span>
    <h2>Player Value--Pitching</h2>    <div class="section_heading_text">
      <ul> <li><a href="/about/war_explained.shtml">WAR Explained (v2.2)</a>: 8+ MVP, 5+ A-S, 2+ Starter, 0-2 Sub, &lt; 0 Repl</li>

         <th aria-label="&lt;strong&gt;Wins Above Avg Adjustment&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;For relief pitchers, we multiply WAA by (1+gmLI)/2. This is done in recognition of the added importance of high leverage. WAA&lt;em&gt;adj&lt;/em&gt; is the additional value of this leverage adjustment. Also, the manner in which this and the WAA calculations are performed cause the league total WAA to move away from zero, so we also do an operation to recenter the entire league. The recentering forces the league sum to 0 which is as it should be for Wins Above Average. So for the league as a whole, WAA+WAA&lt;em&gt;adj&lt;/em&gt; will equal zero and WAR = WAA + WAA&lt;em&gt;adj&lt;/em&gt; + Replacement value" data-stat="WAA_adj" scope="col" class=" poptip center" data-tip="&lt;strong&gt;Wins Above Avg Adjustment&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;For relief pitchers, we multiply WAA by (1+gmLI)/2. This is done in recognition of the added importance of high leverage. WAA&lt;em&gt;adj&lt;/em&gt; is the additional value of this leverage adjustment. Also, the manner in which this and the WAA calculations are performed cause the league total WAA to move away from zero, so we also do an operation to recenter the entire league. The recentering forces the league sum to 0 which is as it should be for Wins Above Average. So for the league as a whole, WAA+WAA&lt;em&gt;adj&lt;/em&gt; will equal zero and WAR = WAA + WAA&lt;em&gt;adj&lt;/em&gt; + Replacement value" >WAAadj</th>

This value includes defensive support and includes additional value for high leverage situations.&lt;br&gt;Scale: 8+ MVP Quality, 5+ All-Star Quality, 2+ Starter,&lt;br&gt;0-2 Reserve, &lt; 0 Replacement Level &lt;br&gt; Developed by Sean Smith of BaseballProjection.com" data-filter="1" data-name="WAR for Pitchers" >WAR</th>

Team&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;This is the win-loss of an otherwise average team in ONLY the games this player played in.&lt;br&gt;For example, for a pitcher this would only consider the games the pitcher threw in and ignoring games they did not play in." >waaWL%</th>
         <th aria-label="&lt;strong&gt;Win-Loss% w/ Avg. Team Season&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;This is the win-loss of an otherwise average team for an entire season giving them credit for only the games this player played in.&lt;br&gt;For example, for a pitcher this would be waaW-L%&lt;br&gt;in the games the pitcher threw in and a .500 record otherwise." data-stat="waa_win_perc_162" scope="col" class=" poptip center" data-tip="&lt;strong&gt;Win-Loss% w/ Avg.          <th aria-label="&lt;strong&gt;Percentage of all hits for extra bases &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;Percentage of all hits resulting in extra bases.&lt;br&gt;(2B + 3B + HR) / H )" data-stat="extra_base_hit_per_hit_perc" scope="col" class=" poptip hide_non_quals center" data-tip="&lt;strong&gt;Percentage of all hits for extra bases &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;Percentage of all hits resulting in extra bases.&lt;br&gt;(2B + 3B + HR) / H )" >X/H%</th>
         <th aria-label="&lt;strong&gt;Ground Ball to Fly Ball Ratio&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;Includes line drives as fly balls.&lt;br&gt;Batted ball type and location is not complete prior to 1988." data-stat="gb_fb_ratio" scope="col" class=" poptip hide_non_quals center" data-tip="&lt;strong&gt;Ground Ball to Fly Ball Ratio&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;Includes line drives as fly balls.&lt;br&gt;Batted ball type and location is not complete prior to 1988." data-filter="1" data-name="&lt;strong&gt;Ground Ball to Fly Ball Ratio&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;Includes line drives as fly balls.&lt;br&gt;Batted ball type and location is not complete prior to 1988." >GB/FB</th>

         <th aria-label="&lt;strong&gt;Balls In-Play Percentage&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;Percentage of all plate appearances with ball put into play.&lt;br&gt;(AB-SO-HR+SF)/(all plate appearances)" data-stat="inplay_perc" scope="col" class=" poptip hide_non_quals center" data-tip="&lt;strong&gt;Balls In-Play Percentage&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;Percentage of all plate appearances with ball put into play.&lt;br&gt;(AB-SO-HR+SF)/(all plate appearances)" data-filter="1" data-name="&lt;strong&gt;Balls In-Play Percentage&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;Percentage of all plate appearances with ball put into play.&lt;br&gt;(AB-SO-HR+SF)/(all plate appearances)" >IP%</th>

<a name="data_completeness"></a>
<strong>*</strong> Many Detailed Statistics are based on play-by-play accounts 
accumulated by <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.retrosheet.org/">RetroSheet</a>.  
These totals may be <a title="summary of missing pbp data by team and year"
href="/about/coverage.shtml">incomplete</a> (3.6% of all plays from 
1930 to 1973 are missing or have incomplete accounts, click 
link for 
<a href="/about/coverage.shtml">year and team summary of data completeness</a>) 
for some players prior to 1974 and even complete seasons may not match the 
official totals due to errors in both the official totals and the play-by-play
accounts. Pre-1954 seasons have a substantial numbers of games missing 
play-by-play accounts and should be viewed as essentially incomplete.
